***doorlopen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doorlopen.html>doorlopen</a> (2567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">door-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doorlopen.html>doorlopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go through, to go from start to end</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doorlopen.html>doorlopen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep going, to move on, to carry on, to continue</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

***doorprikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:doorprikken.html>doorprikken</a> (76332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prikken.html>prikken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doorprikken.html>doorprikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to puncture</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expose as false</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be connected, to be intertwined</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">dōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*daud</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*daudaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="dum">dôot</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>dead</li>
<li>lifeless</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">dōth</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*dauþu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*dauþuz</i>.
</p>

***dork.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dork.html>dork</a> (93987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span></h3>
<p>US 1960s, sense of "silly person" presumably from earlier use as bowdlerization of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dick.html>dick</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in student <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a>, particularly Midwest.<sup id="cite_ref-wo_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-wo-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-oetyld_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-oetyld-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-hdas_4-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-hdas-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>
</p><p>Alternative etymology derives from dialectal <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">dorg</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a mass; heap; a heavy, slovenly woman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dork.html>dork</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">dorks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A quirky, silly and/or stupid, socially inept person, or one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> out of touch with contemporary <a href = vnd.unilang:trends.html>trends</a>. Often confused with <a href = vnd.unilang:nerd.html>nerd</a> and geek, but does not imply the same level of intelligence. <span class="defdate">[from the 20th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1962</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:alain.html>Alain</a> Robbe-Grillet,  <cite>Last year at Marienbad</cite>, page 167:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I entitled the piece "Dorky", <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:dork.html>dork</a></b></i> being <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> for a person who does not belong to popular groups, usually an outsider, an odd person, sometimes inept, other times cranky.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1967</b>, Don Moser and <a href = vnd.unilang:jerry.html>Jerry</a> Cohen, <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:pied.html>Pied</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:piper.html>Piper</a> of Tucson:</i><sup id="cite_ref-wo_1-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-wo-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-hdas_4-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-hdas-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>
<dl><dd>I didn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have any <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> and I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> short hair and looked like a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dork.html>dork</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>Girls</a> wouldn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> go out with <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a>. <span class="defdate">[from the 20th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1962</b>,  Jerome Weidman,  <cite>The Sound of Bow Bells</cite>, page 362:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">As a matter of fact, this slob <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> full of information today. He <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> why <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> Jews have different <b>dorks</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1986</b>,  Stephen King,  <cite>It</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"You’re dead, Trashmouth," <a href = vnd.unilang:vince.html>Vince</a> “Boogers” Taliendo <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> him, pulling his <a href = vnd.unilang:jock.html>jock</a> up <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dork.html>dork</a></b> roughly the size and shape of an anemic peanut.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:mike.html>Mike</a> Judge,  <cite>Reading <a href = vnd.unilang:sucks.html>Sucks</a>: The Collected Works of Beavis and <a href = vnd.unilang:butthead.html>Butthead</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"There's that <a href = vnd.unilang:dork.html>dork</a> whose wife cut off his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dork.html>dork</a></b>." And when people ask him for an autograph he writes, "<a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>Best</a> of luck to Betsy. Signed, the guy whose wife cut off his <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a>."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span></h5>
<p>Narrowly used to indicate someone inept or out of touch, broadly used to mean simply “silly, foolish”; compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">doofus</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">twit</i>.
</p>

<p>Uncertain; apparently from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span></span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dirk.html>dirk</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dirk.html>dirk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a long dagger</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***dorst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dorst.html>dorst</a> (2894)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dorst.html>dorst</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">thurst</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þurstuz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dorst.html>dorst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>thirst, physical need/desire to <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a></li>
<li>thirst, need, longing</li></ol>

***dosis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dosis.html>dosis</a> (5669)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:dosis.html>dosis</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δόσις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dósis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a portion prescribed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a giving</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, used by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galen" class="extiw" title="w:Galen">Galen</a> and other Greek physicians to mean an amount of medicine, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">δίδωμι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dídōmi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to give</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dosis.html>dosis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:doses.html>doses</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dosissen.html>dosissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dosis.html>dosisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dose</span></li></ol>
